 germany ke vittamantri volfgong shaeyubal ne sabhi prakaar kii baatcheet ko prabhavi tareeke se khaarij kar diya or kaha ki ravivaar ko protsaahan paikaj kii sharton par janadesh se pehle koi samjhauta sambhav nahin he
 He said at the Berlin press conference, "first the Greeks have to clarify what they want and then we will talk
" 
 
 ’’ yunaan is samay sankat main fansaa hua he jahaan bank puure saptaah band rahenge
 However, thousands of branches opened today to pay pension to the elderly
 pradhanmantri sipperas ne yunaan ke prastaav ko un sansthaanon ke pramukhon ko bheja jinhone 2010 se europea desh ko mili 240 arab euro ke do protsaahan pakajon kaa prabandh kiya tha
 The government has said that any agreement would allow Greece to maintain a 30 percent VAT exemption on the islands and defer the 2012 pension reform by October 2015
 tippaniyan Greece is seeking a stimulus package of around 30 billion euros for two years to avoid the danger of its separation from the euro area

 5 billion euros (1
 7 arab dollar) ke rin bhugtan main chook karne ke baad protsaahan paikaj kii maang kii he

 The government has said that any agreement would allow Greece to maintain a 30 percent VAT exemption on the islands and defer the 2012 pension reform by October 2015
 tippaniyan Greece is seeking a stimulus package of around 30 billion euros for two years to avoid the danger of its separation from the euro area

 5 billion euros (1
 7 arab dollar) ke rin bhugtan main chook karne ke baad protsaahan paikaj kii maang kii he
 Germany's Finance Minister Wolfgang Schaeuble effectively rejected all types of negotiations, saying that no agreement is possible before the mandate on the terms of the stimulus packages on Sunday
 unhone berlin samvaadadaata sammelan main kaha, ‘‘sabase pehle yunaan ko apni sthiti spasht kerani hogi aakhir vah kya chahta he or tab uske baad ham baatcheet karenge
 
 
 Greece is currently in a crisis where banks will remain closed all week
 haalanki bujurgon ko pension ke bhugtan ke liye aaj kareeb hajaaron shakhaaen khuli
 Prime Minister Sipres sent the Greek proposal to the heads of the institutions that had managed two stimulus packages worth EUR 240 billion to the European country since 2010
 sarkaar ne kaha he ki kisi bhi samjhaute main yunaan ko dwipon par 30 pratishat waite chhot ko banaaye rakhane tathaa 2012 pension sudhaar ko aktubar 2015 tak taale jane kii anumati deni hogi

 yunaan ne imef ko 1
 5 billion euros (1
 7 arab dollar) ke rin bhugtan main chook karne ke baad protsaahan paikaj kii maang kii he
 The Indian team, led by new coach and captain Sunil Chhetri, completed the title hat-trick by defeating Cameroon on Sunday in the final of the Nehru Cup football tournament
 penalty shoot out tak chale is mukaable main bhartiya team ne 5-4 se jeet darj kii
 The match played at the Jawaharlal Nehru Stadium in the capital ended in a 2–2 draw in the stipulated time
 iske baad khele gaye aadhe ghante ke atirikt samay main mukaable main bhi donon main koi bhi team gol nahin kar saki or match 2-2 kii barabari par rahane ke kaaran penalty shoot out main pahunch gaya
 India scored five of the five goals in the penalty shootout, while Cameroon's team scored four goals and eventually went in India's favor
 is final mukaable main pehla gol bharat ne kiya
 Gaurmangi Singh scored from India in the 19th minute through a brilliant header and gave India a 1-0 lead
 lekin bhartiya team abhi jeet kaa jashn manaane main hi lagi thi ki camerun ne gol dagkar mukaable ko 1-1 kii barabari par pahunchaa diya
 After this, Cameroon scored another goal and disappointed in the Indian camp
 lekin bhartiya khilaadiyon ne ummid nahin chodi
 In the second half, India played aggressively and scored a penalty in the 79th minute of the game to take the match to 2–2
 nirdhaarit samay kaa khel samaapt hone tak donon timen 2-2 kii barabari par rahi
 This was followed by an extra match of half an hour
 is dauraan camerun team ne aakraamak rukh akhriyaar karte hue ek ke baad ek hamale kiye lekin bhartiya rakshapankti ne in hamalon ko naakaam kar diya
 In extra time too, the match ended at 2-2
 muqabla penalty shoot out main pahunchaa
 Robin Singh, Sunil Chhetri, Denzil Franco, Mehtab Hussain and Clifford Marandi converted their respective goals into goals for India but the final penalty shoot by Cameroon could not turn into a goal and eventually a thrilling match
 Ended with India's victory
 bhartiya team ke captain sunil chhetri ne is pratiyogita main kul paanch gol daage
 He was adjudged the best player of the competition along with the final match for this performance
 final se pehle donon timen lig str par jab pehali baar bhidi to camerun ne usamen baaji maari thi
 Cameroon defeated the hosts 1-0 in the final round robin league match played on Friday
 donon tiimon kii fifa ranking main kaaphi antar he
 Cameroon is 59th while India is 168th
 bharat is paanch deshon ke aamantran toornament ko 2007 or 2009 main apane naam kar chukaa tha or 2012 ko apane naam kar usne khitaabi hetric puri kii
 Both times Indian team Drs
 ambedkar stadium main champion bani thi jabaki is baar maidan doosraa tha
 New coach of the Indian team, Vim Koevermans expressed happiness over the team's performance and said that there are high expectations from this team
 unhone kaha ki bharat main footbal kaa bhavishya ujjwal he basharte ki yahaan ke khilaadiyon ko suvidhaayen uplabdh hon
 At the league level, India played a total of four matches, of which they won two, while one match was a draw, while in one match they had to face defeat
 saat ankon ke saath bhartiya team final main pahunchi thi
 The comments camerun ne apane chaar maichon main se teen main jeet darj kiye the jabaki ek match uskaa dra rahaa
 Cameron qualified for the final with 10 points topping the points table
 bharat ne lig str par apane pehle mukaable main pichley baar kii up vijeta syria ko 2-1 se parajeet kiya jabaki maldive ko usne 3-0 se shikast di
 India's match with Nepal ended in a goalless draw while Cameron defeated India 1-0 in the final league match
 rajdhani ke jawaharlal nehru stadium main khelaa gaya yah muqabla nirdhaarit samay main 2-2 kii barabari par samaapt hua
 After this, in the half-hour extra time played, neither team could score a goal in both matches and the match reached the penalty shootout as the match was 2–2
 penalty shootout main bharat ne paanch main se paanch gol daage jabaki camerun kii team chaar hi gol daag saki or antat: muqabla bharat ke paksh main gaya
 India scored the first goal in this final match
 bharat kii ore se gauramangi singh ne 19wein minute main shandaar header ke jariye gol daaga or bharat ko 1-0 kii badhat dilaai
 But the Indian team was still in the process of celebrating the victory that Cameroon scored the goal to make it 1-1
 iske baad camerun ne ek or gol dagkar bhartiya kheme main niraash failaa di
 But the Indian players did not give up hope
 duusare half main bharat ne aakraamak khel dikhaaya or khel ke 79wein minute main mili penalty ke jariye gol kar mukaable ko 2-2 kii barabari par pahunchaa diya
 Both teams were tied at 2–2 until the scheduled play ended
 iske baad aadhe ghante kaa atirikt match hua
 During this time, the Cameroon team made aggressive attacks one after the other, but the Indian defense thwarted these attacks
 atirikt samay main bhi muqabla 2-2 kii barabari par hi samaapt hua
 The bout reached the penalty shootout
 bharat kii ore se robin singh, sunil chhetri, denzil franco, mehtab hossain or clifford marandi ne apane-apane maukon ko gol main tabdeel kiya lekin camerun kii ore se lagaaya gaya antim penalty shoot gol main tabdeel nahin ho sakaa or antat: ek romaanchak mukaable kaa ant bharat kii jeet ke saath samaapt hua
 Indian team captain Sunil Chhetri scored a total of five goals in this competition
 unhen is pradarshan ke liye final match ke saath-saath pratiyogita kaa sarvshereshth khilaadi ghoshit kiya gaya
 Before the final, when both teams clashed for the first time at the league level, Cameroon won it
 shuukravaar ko khele gaye antim round robin lig mukaable main camerun ne mejabaan team ko 1-0 se haraaya tha
 There is a big difference in the FIFA rankings of the two teams
 camerun 59wein jabaki bharat 168wein sthaan par he
 India had won this five-nation invitational tournament in 2007 and 2009 and completed the title hat-trick in 2012
 donon baar bhartiya team dow
 Ambedkar became the champion in the stadium while the field was second this time
 bhartiya team ke nae coach vim kovermans team pradarshan par khushi jataate hue kaha ki is team se kaaphi ummiden hai

 Arvind Panagarhiyah, the first Deputy Chairman of the NITI Aayog constituted by the Modi government, is a pro-economist of the open market
 america ke colombia vishvavidhyalay ke 62 varshiya professor panagadhiya ‘aarthik vruddhi hasil karne ke liye gujarat model ke prakhar samarthak rahe hai
 Know ahead 7 special things about Panagarhia
 1
 indian-american economist Panagaria is a close associate of economist Jagdish Bhagwati, a scholar of world trade
 donon ne hi bhartiya arthvyavastha ke bare main nobel puraskaar vijeta amartya sen ke vichaaron ko khuli chunauti di he
 2
 pradhanmantri narendra modi ke rashtriya kshitij par ubharne ke pehle se hi panagadhiya gujarat ke mukhyamantri ke rup main modi kii aarthik nitiyon kaa samarthan karte rahe the
 The book is India's Trust with Destiny, jointly written by Panagadhiya and Bhagwati
 is kitaab main ‘‘gujarat model’’ kaa jumala istemaal kiya gaya
 Which is the epitome of such a model of development, is mainly a model to achieve the goals of development by increasing high growth and private entrepreneurship
 in donon ne ‘kerala ke vikaas namoonay’ ko praathmik taur par punarvitaran or rajya dwaara chalaae jane vaala vikaas model bataaya
 3
 pichley saal sampann loksabhaa chunaavon ke dauraan modi ke gujarat model ko unki party ne apana mukhya agenda banaaya
 Sen said at the time that India should invest more on social infrastructure projects to boost people's productivity for economic growth
 america ke princetone vishvavidhyalay se piechdi degree dharak panagadhiya vruddhi ko badhaava dene ke liye adhik puunji vyay ke bhi samarthak rahe hai
 He has also been advocating loosening the fiscal deficit target
 4
 Currently a professor of economics at Columbia University, Panagadia was also the Chief Economist of the Asian Development Bank before that
 vah college park, maryland uniwarsity ke antarrashtriya arthshaastra kendra main professor or sah-nideshak ke rup main bhi kaam kar chuke hai
 5
 arthshaastra ke is professor ne vishwabank, antarrashtriya mudrakosh, vishwa vyapaar sanghathan or vyapaar evam vikaas ke sanyukt raashtra sammelan (ankatad) main bhi vibhinn padon par kaary kiya he
 Panagadhia did her graduation from Rajasthan University and has written 15 books on economic growth with Jagdish Bhagwati
 6
 The government has also earlier honored Padma Bhushan with Arvind Panagarhia
 rajasthan kii vasundhara raaje sarkaar main salaahkaar rahe panagadhiya ko rajya main shram sudhaaron kaa bada samarthak mana jaataa he

V
 ke
 Saraswat has also been appointed as a member of the Commission
 7
 Educated from Cambridge, Debroy has held various positions in the Government of India
 debaroy rajeev gandhi institute for contemparari studies ke nideshak bhi rah chuke hai
 Advisor in the Department of Economic Affairs in the Ministry of Finance and phd has also been Secretary General of the Board of Industries 
 saraswat, bhartiya vaigyanik hai or raksha mantri ke mukhya vaigyanik salaahkaar bhi rah chuke hai

 tomars ko giraftaar kiya or unhen pad se istipha dena padaa
 Remind you, then Chief Minister Kejriwal defended Tomar, but when Tomar could not prove his innocence in the court, he had to resign
 us vakt kai netaaon kii degree ko lekar sawaal uth rahe the, magar unke maamle main tomars jaisi tatparta nahin dikhaai gai
 It is obvious that the Aam Aadmi Party and Chief Minister Kejriwal were getting aggressive in raising the matter of the Prime Minister's degree, as they found Delhi Police active in Tomar's case
 aam aadmi party ke netaa sakriyata se twit kar rahe the
 He was challenging and asking for the Prime Minister's degree, stating his degree
 maamle ko aupchaarik manyata tab mil gai jab 29 april ko kendriya soochna ayukta ne piemo or dilli vishvavidhyalay ko nirdesh diya ki pradhanmantri kii degree kii jaankaree uplabdh karai jaae
 i do not know whether the University of Delhi and the PMO have given any information about the degree
 lekin somvaar ko bijepi ke rashtriya adhyaksh amit shah or vitt mantri arun jetali ne press conference kiya or pradhanmantri kii bie or eme kii degree jari kar di
 What would BJP also do
 itane sawaal uth rahe the ki jawaab dena hi padaa, lekin agar dilli vishvavidhyalay ne apni taraf se jawaab de diya hota to is vishay ke liye in do mahatvapurn vyaktiyon ko apana samay nahin barbaad karnaa padataa
 In the press conference convened at 1 pm on Monday, Amit Shah and Arun Jaitley showed the Prime Minister's degree and said that Kejriwal has maligned the name of the country
 ve iske liye sabase maafee maangen
 The Prime Minister passed his BA from Delhi University in 1978 in the third category
 1983 main gujarat vishvavidhyalay se prathan shrenee main eme kii degree di gai
 The BJP has also released the Prime Minister's mark sheet, so that there is no scope of accusation
 arun jetali ne bataaya ki jis dashak main pradhanmantri ne degree hasil kii he, us samay desh main apatkaal laga tha
 The Prime Minister used to come from Gujarat to Delhi for examination
 arvind kejariwal ne tathyon kii jaanch kiye bagaiyr itnaa bada maamla bana diya
 The Aam Aadmi Party has taken it very seriously
 isliye ab uski javaabadari he ki is masale par apane tathy rakhe yaa isse kinaaraa kare
 Ashutosh came after the BJP press conference and he held a counter press conference
 ashutosh ne kaha ki amit shah or arun jetali koi bhagwaan nahin hai ki wo bol denge to janata maan legi
 Ashutosh challenged that Amit Shah and Arun Jaitley present the affidavit
 ashutosh ne bie kii degree par pradhanmantri ke naam or eme kii degree par likhe naam ke antar ke aadhaar par daawa kiya ki degree farzi he
 i have my own opinion on this
 digriyon main naamon kii chapai main galati ho jaati he
 Happens to millions of people
 kuch log samay par thik kara lete hai or kuch log kai kaarnon se yaa to thik hi nahin karaate yaa bahut baad main karaate hai
 Therefore, on the basis of this matter, Ashutosh's talk was weak
 iske baad ashutosh ne kaha ki marksheet par 1977 likhaa he
 Wrote 1978 on BA degree
 ab pataa chalaa he ki 1977 main pradhanmantri fail ho gaye
 He only got 473 numbers in 1200
 lekin 1978 main ve paas ho gaye
 In 1200, 489 numbers came
 1977 kii tulana main 1978 main 16 number zyaada aae
 i feel bad that someone's number is being discused in public like this, that too of the Prime Minister
 phir bhi aam aadmi party aakraamak he
 Ashutosh has invited Amit Shah and Arun Jaitley to go to Delhi University
 donon milakar kaagazat jaanchenge

 inke paas mukhyamantri kejariwal kaa athurity letters tha, jisamen kendriya soochna ayog ne piem modi kii degree kii jaankaree kejariwal ko dene kaa aadesh diya tha
 Chief Minister Kejriwal transferred his authority to these three leaders
 vahaan par ye teenon ek ghanta rahe

 AAP leaders will again visit Delhi University on Tuesday

 BJP has presented fake documents in the press conference
 kendriya soochna ayukta ke aadesh ko lagu kiya jaae or isaki jaanch kii anumati milani chahie
 Ideally, the University of Delhi should have been informed about this dispute by now, as the Gujarat University did
 gujarat vishvavidlaay ne unki degree jari kar bataa diya ki 1983 pratham shrenee main eme paas hue hai
 Now a question is being raised that the Prime Minister's degree has written Antire Political Science
 aam aadmi party ke netaa kehete hai ki antair polytical science kii degree to kabhi dekhi nahin, suni nahin
 Our colleague Rajiv Pathak has told that in Gujarat, first the degree of full state science was available
 gujarati main polytical science ko rajya shaastra kehete hai
 In Hindi regions, it is called political science
 shukr he ki kisi ne yah nahin kaha ki raajnneeti shaastra to suna he rajya shaastra kya hota he
 Otherwise, he would get trapped
 antair polytical science kaa masalaa aap samaj gaye honge
 If you have not studied any subsidiary subject with political science, then you would have got such a degree
 ek hi vishay ke saare paper padhane par sampurna rajya shaastra kii degree milti thi
 Kejriwal not only raised the issue but also took pressure on other parties as to why he was not speaking
 congress to prabhaav main aakar degree kii baat karne lagi, magar bihar ke mukhyamantri nitish kumaar ne is vivaad se khud ko dur kar liya
 Actually everyone has played the game of degree and name dispute
 2005 main subramnian swami supreme court chale gaye ki adaalat chunaav ayog ko sonia gandhi ke kilaaf shikaayat darj karne ko kahe
 According to Swamy, Sonia Gandhi had given incorrect information about her degree in the 2004 affidavit
 12 april 2005 ke hindu akhbaar kii report ke anusaar da swami ne cambridge vishvavidhyalay se jab sonia gandhi kii degree ke bare main poocha to bataaya gaya ki wo kabhi chaatr nahin rahi hai
 Swamy had also alleged that the certificate course mentioned by Sonia in English can be found at any English teaching shop in Cambridge
 supreme court ne swami kii yachika khaarij kar di
 The Supreme Court said that when Sonia Gandhi did not hide any information, then what should be ordered
 tab swami main bijepi main nahin the

 swami ab zarur bijepi main hai or rajya sabha ke sadsy bane hai
 Swamy has raised this issue many times even after the Supreme Court order
 van india website ke anusaar 14 july, 2015 ke din swami ne bengaluru main sonia kii degree kaa maamla uthaaya tha jiskaa you tub par baqayda video maujuud he
 Swamy said that Sonia Gandhi had only studied up to class five
 sonia gandhi ne apane halafname main kaha he ki cambridge uniwarsity se pi ech di kii he

 sonia gandhi bhi aam aadmi party ke netaa jitendra singh tomars kii tarah jail ja sakati hai

 swami bhi sonia gandhi ko tomars kii tarah jail bhejne kii baat kar chuke hai

 is bich yah khabar ai he ki madhyapradesh ke bijepi ke vidhayak moti kashyap kii sadsyta jane kii naubat aa gai he

 fadanviske alaava 7 cabinet or 2 rajya mantri bhi shapath lenge

 shapath grahan samaaroh ke liye kareeb 30 hajaar mehmaanon ko nyotaa bheja gaya he

 Shyama Prasad Mukherjee Civic Center, the headquarters of the MCD, is counted as the tallest building in Delhi, but when we reached the highest floor of this building, we were surprised to see the picture of Delhi, because far more
 Only a thick sheet of pollution was visible
 dilli kaa civik centre conot place ke ekadam nazadik he

 laga jaise seepi gaayab ho gaya he, yahi haal nai dilli railway stesan kaa he

 puraani dilli kaa khubasurat najaare ko bhidhundh kii chadarne dhank liya

 mana ja rahaa he ki congress ke varisht netaa dike sivakumar ne pradesh adhyaksh yaa netaa vipaksh ke pad par daawa kar diya he
 Earlier, Chief Minister Siddaramaiah is considered angry
 siddharmaiya kisi bhi surat main karnataka main dike sivakumar kaa raajnneetik kad badaye jane ke paksh main nahin he
